         <article class="article-card article-card--two-column article-card--no-meta-top article-card--no-excerpt--sm-down" data-article-id="e4781ecb-5c5c-4401-8a76-1cfce970c155" data-category-colour="opinion" data-evt="click" data-evt-typ="User Interaction Click" data-evt-val="{&quot;control_fields&quot;: {&quot;mparticle&quot;: {&quot;keys&quot;: {&quot;Click Source Type&quot;: &quot;Click Source Type&quot;, &quot;Click Source Name&quot;: &quot;Click Source Name&quot;, &quot;Click Source Feed Name&quot;: &quot;Click Source Feed Name&quot;, &quot;Click Source List ID&quot;: &quot;Click Source List ID&quot;, &quot;Click Target URL&quot;: &quot;Click Target URL&quot;, &quot;Click Target Title&quot;: &quot;Click Target Title&quot;, &quot;Click Target ID&quot;: &quot;Click Target ID&quot;, &quot;Click Target Story Position&quot;: &quot;Click Target Story Position&quot;}, &quot;mp_event_type&quot;: &quot;Navigation&quot;, &quot;extra_keys&quot;: [&quot;Click Source Vertical Position %&quot;, &quot;Click Source Vertical Position Pixels&quot;]}}, &quot;Click Source Type&quot;: &quot;widget-list&quot;, &quot;Click Source Name&quot;: &quot;index&quot;, &quot;Click Source Feed Name&quot;: &quot;opinion&quot;, &quot;Click Source List ID&quot;: &quot;e23f1fd0-10d9-4d4c-802b-9a6110d113a2&quot;, &quot;Click Target URL&quot;: &quot;https://edmontonjournal.com/opinion/letters/saturdays-letters-freedom-of-religion-not-an-absolute-right&quot;, &quot;Click Target Title&quot;: &quot;Saturday's letters: Freedom of religion not an absolute right&quot;, &quot;Click Target ID&quot;: &quot;e4781ecb-5c5c-4401-8a76-1cfce970c155&quot;, &quot;Click Target Story Position&quot;: &quot;1&quot;}">
          <div class="article-card__content">
           <div class="article-card__details">
            <div class="article-card__meta-top">
             <span class="article-card__category">
              <a class="article-card__category-link" href="/category/letters/">
               <span>
                Letters
               </span>

            <a aria-label="Saturday's letters: Freedom of religion not an absolute right" class="article-card__link" href="/opinion/letters/saturdays-letters-freedom-of-religion-not-an-absolute-right">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Saturday's letters: Freedom of religion not an absolute right">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Saturday's letters: Freedom of religion not an absolute right
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              Not for the first time, I find myself in disagreement with the case made by John Carpay whose current position as president of the Justice Centre for Constitutional Freedoms has him appearing to suggest that freedom of religion is protected in the Charter of Rights and Freedoms as though it is an “absolute right.” He appears to ignore the fact that all rights in the Charter, including freedom of religion, can be limited by reasonable laws which can be justifiably sustained in a democracy.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__author">
              Edmonton Journal
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__time">
              1 day ago
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__category">
              <a class="article-card__category-link" href="/category/letters/">
               <span>
                Letters
               </span>
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <a aria-label="Saturday's letters: Freedom of religion not an absolute right" class="article-card__image-link" href="/opinion/letters/saturdays-letters-freedom-of-religion-not-an-absolute-right" tabindex="-1">
            <picture class="article-card__image">
             <source data-srcset="https://smartcdn.prod.postmedia.digital/edmontonjournal/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/coates-followers-2-1.jpg?quality=90&amp;strip=all&amp;w=344&amp;type=webp,
            https://smartcdn.prod.postmedia.digital/edmontonjournal/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/coates-followers-2-1.jpg?quality=90&amp;strip=all&amp;w=688&amp;type=webp 2x" media="(min-width: 1200px)" srcset="data:,1w" type="image/webp"/>
             <source data-srcset="https://smartcdn.prod.postmedia.digital/edmontonjournal/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/coates-followers-2-1.jpg?quality=90&amp;strip=all&amp;w=344&amp;type=jpg,

            <a aria-label="Opinion: Post-secondary education has never been more vital to Alberta's future" class="article-card__link" href="/opinion/columnists/opinion-post-secondary-education-has-never-been-more-vital-to-albertas-future">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Opinion: Post-secondary education has never been more vital to Alberta's future">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Opinion: Post-secondary education has never been more vital to Alberta's future
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              For most of the last half-century, Alberta’s governments have understood that our entire province benefits when the post-secondary sector thrives. From Ernest Manning to Peter Lougheed, provincial leaders built a post-secondary system prioritizing excellence and potential for innovation in ways that were almost unmatched for a jurisdiction of Alberta’s size.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__author">
              Joel Agarwal
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__time">
              1 day ago
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__category">
              <a class="article-card__category-link" href="/category/columnists/">
               <span>
                Columnists
               </span>
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>

             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Three to See Saturday: SkirtsAfire extended, Ann Vriend sings and the MCU returns">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Three to See Saturday: SkirtsAfire extended, Ann Vriend sings and the MCU returns
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              Makings of a Voice : This SkirtsAfire Reimagined production has been extended through Saturday, a theatrical song cycle about discovering individual identity within mother and daughter, generational narratives. A mix of music and monologue, this intimate piece follows a messy trajectory into the heart of one woman’s story and provides a compelling argument for why our stories need to be told. The fest’s visual art display Systemic Contradictions // Covid Collections is also still up in the old Army &amp; Navy at 10411 82 Ave. through March 31, as well — some really nice work there, especially Raneece Buddan’s wood sculpture, I Stand as Two, no charge to peek in the windows.
             </p>

            <a aria-label="Under the watch of three gigantic chickadees, CO*LAB is set to GLOW in the Quarters" class="article-card__link" href="/entertainment/festivals/under-the-watch-of-three-gigantic-chickadees-colab-is-set-to-glow-in-the-quarters">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Under the watch of three gigantic chickadees, CO*LAB is set to GLOW in the Quarters">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Under the watch of three gigantic chickadees, CO*LAB is set to GLOW in the Quarters
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              Every spring, Edmonton’s chickadees go from feeding together in territorial winter flocks to disbanding off into pairs to do some things also done by bees your parents can perhaps explain to you.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-middle">
             <span class="article-card__video">
              <span aria-hidden="true" class="article-card__video-icon">
               <svg height="10" viewbox="0 0 16 10" width="16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                <path d="m11.1 2.6v-1.8c0-.4-.4-.8-.8-.8h-9.5c-.4 0-.8.4-.8.8v8.4c0 .4.4.8.8.8h9.5c.4 0 .8-.4.8-.8v-1.8l4.9 2.6v-10z">
                </path>
               </svg>
              </span>
              <span class="article-card__video-text">
               with Video
